[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapproximately [0m[1;36m28[0m[39m seconds while processing a TAR archive. The timeout occurred in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe Java BigDecimal division routines triggered by PAX header parsing in the Apache[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCommons Compress library.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer entry point [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`CompressTarFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m constructs a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`TarFile` instance and reads entries.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- During PAX header processing [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`TarArchiveEntry.processPaxHeader` → [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the code invokes `BigDecimal.divide` and related[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethods deep in the `java.math` package.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The thread dump shows the “main” thread stuck in [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MutableBigInteger.divideOneWord` and higher-level `BigDecimal` division methods [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor over [0m[1;36m26[0m[39m seconds.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No explicit vulnerability type [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., crash, overflow[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is mentioned; the issue [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmanifests as a performance hang [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtimeout[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The method `parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds` in `TarArchiveEntry` uses `new [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mBigDecimal[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvalue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and subsequent `[0m[1;35m.remainder[0m[1;39m([0m[39mBigDecimal.ONE[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.movePointRight[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m9[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations on the entire fractional string. Because the regex [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`PAX_EXTENDED_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_FILE_TIMES_PATTERN` only bounds the integer part [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m19[0m[39m digits[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut leaves the fractional part unbounded [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`\d*`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, malicious or fuzzed inputs with [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvery long fractional parts trigger pathological performance in `BigDecimal.divide` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand related routines. This is what causes the fuzzer timeout.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve Existing Logic[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must continue to:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Accept valid PAX‐style timestamps including optional fractional seconds.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Preserve up to nanosecond precision [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m9[0m[39m decimal digits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Throw `IOException` only when the format is invalid [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnot for legitimately [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformatted values[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must not alter harness or utility code; only the `TarArchiveEntry` source.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Restrict the number of allowed fractional digits via the existing regex so [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat only values with at most [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m digits after the decimal point pass validation.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Change the pattern from[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         `-?\d[0m[1;39m{[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m19[0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m([0m[39m?:\.\d*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m?`[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        to[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         `-?\d[0m[1;39m{[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m19[0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m([0m[39m?:\.\d[0m[1;39m{[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m9[0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m?`[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This ensures:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • Integers [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno dot[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m19[0m[39m digits.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         • If a dot appears, there may be zero to nine digits after it—no more.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Any value with more than nine fractional digits will fail `[0m[1;35m.matches[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately throw an `IOException`, avoiding expensive `BigDecimal` work.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptional [0m[35m/[0m[39m future enhancement[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m If the project prefers to accept arbitrarily [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlong fractional digits by truncating rather than rejecting:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. In `parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds`, after validating the format, split on[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe `[0m[32m'.'[0m[39m`.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Truncate or pad the fractional substring to exactly nine digits.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Parse the integral part with `Long.parseLong`, compute nanoseconds by [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mLong.parseLong[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtruncatedFraction[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, apply sign, and call [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mInstant.ofEpochSecond[0m[1;39m([0m[39mseconds, nanos[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Remove or bypass the use of `BigDecimal` entirely for the fractional [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextraction.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This approach avoids throwing exceptions for >[0m[1;36m9[0m[39m fractional digits and still[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcaps the workload to a fixed small scale.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Steps to Implement[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. In [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/tar/TarArchiveEntry.java`, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocate the pattern declaration:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         private static final Pattern PAX_EXTENDED_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_FILE_TIMES_PATTERN =[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"-?\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,19[0m[32m}[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.\\d*[0m[32m)[0m[32m?"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Update it to:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         private static final Pattern PAX_EXTENDED_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39mER_FILE_TIMES_PATTERN =[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"-?\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,19[0m[32m}[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m0,9[0m[32m}[0m[32m)[0m[32m?"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Leave the rest of `parseInstantFromDecimalSeconds` unchanged. With the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrestricted regex, any input reaching the `BigDecimal` logic will be at most [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfractional digits, eliminating the performance hang.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Add or update unit tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39moutside the harness[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to cover:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Valid values with [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m9[0m[39m fractional digits [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `[0m[32m"42"[0m[39m`, `[0m[32m"42.123456789"[0m[39m`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[32m"-3.5"[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Invalid values: more than [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m digits after the dot [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `[0m[32m"0.1234567890"[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto ensure they trigger the `IOException`.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By bounding the fractional digits at [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m, we directly prevent the pathological [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mworkloads in the `BigDecimal.divide` and related methods without touching harness [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor utility code.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This respects the existing API contract: valid PAX timestamps up to nanosecond[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprecision remain accepted; invalid formats remain rejected.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The regex change is minimal, low-risk, and maintains linear‐time validation in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe regex engine, which is far cheaper than arbitrary‐precision division on huge [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minputs.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side-Effects & Mitigation[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Side-effect: Inputs with more than [0m[1;36m9[0m[39m fractional digits now cause an [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`IOException` rather than an Instant truncated or rounded silently.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mitigation: If users truly require more precision, they can post-process raw [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheader values or request a feature. Alternatively, implement the optional [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtruncation approach in a later release.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No tests or harness code are modified, so existing tests should still pass. [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mEnsure new unit tests capture the intended behavior.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/tar/TarArchiveEntry.jav[0m[1;92ma:221[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m22[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
